(installfiles=`echo ./html/*.sgml ./html/*.html ./html/*.png ./html/*.css`; \
if test "$installfiles" = './html/*.sgml ./html/*.html ./html/*.png ./html/*.css'; \
then echo '-- Nothing to install' ; \
else \
  /bin/sh /tmp/gst-plugins-base/src/gst-plugins-base-1.6.0/install-sh -d /tmp/gst-plugins-base/pkg/gst-plugins-base-libs/usr/share/gtk-doc/html/gst-plugins-base-libs-1.0; \
  for i in $installfiles; do \
    echo '-- Installing '$i ; \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $i /tmp/gst-plugins-base/pkg/gst-plugins-base-libs/usr/share/gtk-doc/html/gst-plugins-base-libs-1.0; \
  done; \
  echo '-- Installing ./html/gst-plugins-base-libs-1.0.devhelp2' ; \
  if test -e ./html/gst-plugins-base-libs-1.0.devhelp2; then \
            /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./html/gst-plugins-base-libs-1.0.devhelp2 \
            /tmp/gst-plugins-base/pkg/gst-plugins-base-libs/usr/share/gtk-doc/html/gst-plugins-base-libs-1.0/gst-plugins-base-libs-1.0.devhelp2; \
  fi; \
  true --relative --dest-dir=/tmp/gst-plugins-base/pkg/gst-plugins-base-libs --html-dir=/tmp/gst-plugins-base/pkg/gst-plugins-base-libs/usr/share/gtk-doc/html/gst-plugins-base-libs-1.0 || true ; \
fi)
